name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Premier Room - Garden-View
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted August 10, 2023
msg:Let me start with the conclusion: Treasure Hotel is great value for money! ! A hotel suitable for two or three days with children (especially when going to the west slope of Tianchi)

Reason: I booked it temporarily. I wanted to stay for a day between North Slope and West Slope. I didn't expect it to be an unexpected surprise. As a result, I checked out of the hotel in Wanda Town and stayed again. It can be said that it is the most convenient hotel to visit Xipo Tianchi. It is located in Baixi Town between Xipo Distribution Center and the mountain entrance.

The hotel hardware is rated 4.8 stars, the service is 4.5 stars, the price is similar to that of a 3.5 star hotel, and the price/performance ratio is high.

Personal experience: For the hotel closest to the west slope of Tianchi, you can get a certificate at the front desk and go directly to the entrance to buy a ticket. Not only is a ticket discount of 14 yuan, but the most important thing is that there is a dedicated entrance to the hotel in Baixi Town. You can go there halfway and you don‚Äôt have to. Go to the visitor center and wait in long lines to save time. We took our two children to slowly climb Tianchi and the canyon. We started from the hotel at 7:30 in the morning, entered the mountain pass at 8:00, and went to the parking lot at the foot of Tianchi at 9:10 to start climbing. At 2 p.m., we returned to the hotel from Tianchi. After rest, go rafting.

We came here from Bei Slope. Tianyu is also the West Slope Hotel closest to Bei Slope. It is on the side of Huanshan Road, about 75 kilometers away from Bei Slope. The Didi Express is less than 200 yuan and it takes about an hour to drive there. It takes 20 minutes, and the whole journey is a forest road with beautiful scenery. It takes about 15 minutes by bus from the mountain entrance on the west slope of Tianchi, which is about half the distance closer than those hotels in Wanda Town.

The hotel's breakfast is not particularly rich in variety, but the taste is good. The chef's level is above four stars, far exceeding the level of hotels in the same price range in Changbai Mountain, and it only costs RMB 68 for one extra person, which is a great value.

Let‚Äôs talk about the advantages and disadvantages in detail:
shortcoming:
1) The surrounding area is relatively remote and seems a bit deserted due to the low occupancy rate. But the hotel itself has a very good natural environment, surrounded by woods and small ponds on boardwalks.
2) The glass is dirty and needs to be wiped!

Dining guide: The hotel has breakfast and dinner. For dinner, there are four 198 set meals to choose from. Add a few bowls of rice to feed four people. The pot-wrapped pork is delicious. More than 300 meters away from the hotel, there is a home-cooked dish from Jiashan Girl, which can be used for lunch. Although the price is not cheap, the Northeastern cuisine is surprisingly large, fresh, tastes home-cooked, and they also provide takeaway;

Advantages of Tianyu:
1) The room is large, basically 40 to 50 square meters, with a sofa and computer with Internet access. The bathroom is large, with double washbasins and a separate bathtub to relieve fatigue; 2) The bedding is comfortable and clean; 3) The hotel has its own hot spring, although it is only There are two large pools, but they are very clean, the water quality is clear, and it is a bit Japanese style. It is a pity that there is no small courtyard landscape. The water temperature is comfortable for soaking. The outdoor pool is ventilated and comfortable and you can watch the stars. It is simply a life-saving pool after climbing the 1442 Tianchi steps; 4 ) The hotel has a European-style appearance, and it is very photogenic. You can take pictures of the forest and clouds in the yard; 5) The front desk guarantees all services, and the big-eyed guy is very considerate (I heard that he was transferred from Sanya Tianyu and received training The service is really good); 6) There are many facilities for children, including two outdoor children's equipment and an indoor small amusement park, where you can also play with rabbits; 7) Baixi rafting in front of the hotel, the cooperation price is only 40 yuan per person, and you can float one hour, there is also a car pick-up, which is a great deal. We also did the first rafting in the primitive ecology. The water flow was fast. Although it was exciting, it took more than 30 minutes to complete the rafting, and the price doubled. My husband said that the scenery in Baixi is better and smoother, and you can lie on the water and watch the blue sky.

A few additional words: Before booking, I read Ctrip reviews. There were a lot of bad reviews in July, so I didn‚Äôt have high expectations. However, I didn‚Äôt encounter the problems mentioned above when I checked in from August 8 to 10. I guess it may be because it has not been open during the epidemic. When it first opened in July, the facilities had some musty smell and rust in the water.

msg:The hotel is very close to the airport, there is a small supermarket and gas station within 200 meters
The service is very good, the staff is very friendly to children
Tianyu has always focused on parent-child, indoor and outdoor amusement parks (because there are few people, it is almost a private room, and children are very satisfied), mini zoos, rocking cars, riding dogs and other basic amusement facilities.
There are very few people in summer, and the crowds of people drinking Sanya Tianyu are not at the same level
Because of the small number of people, although there are not many types of breakfast, it is exquisite; for dinner, there are indoor ordering and outdoor campfire barbecues. There are not many types but enough, and the blind spots of taste are very good (some fungus mushrooms are grown by themselves, which can be seen from the parking lot. fresh and tasty)
The only fly in the oin**ent is the location. There are no attractions and restaurants nearby, and there are no supporting buildings around. It is very barren
It is suitable for families who drive by themselves in summer, because the Changbai Mountain scenic spot is already very scattered, it doesn‚Äôt matter if you have a car, and it is not recommended if you don‚Äôt have a car; there is no ski resort nearby in winter, and it takes more than 20 minutes to drive to Wanda Luneng.
